<?php
// Font Awesome v. 5

function geodir_font_awesome_array() {
	$wp_font_awesome = WP_Font_Awesome_Settings::instance();
	$settings = $wp_font_awesome->get_settings();

	$free_icons = geodir_font_awesome_free_array();

	if ( ! empty( $settings['pro'] ) ) {
		$icons = array_merge( geodir_font_awesome_pro_array(), $free_icons );
	} else {
		$icons = $free_icons;
	}

	return $icons;
}
